Single Method

For being afflicted by poison: Wheat flour powder, take two cups of wheat flour, divide into three doses, and mix with cold water. Take all within half a day, and the poison will be expelled, leading to recovery.

To antidote poison: Fresh turtle shell juice, drink a cup with water, and it will dissolve the poison.

Various poisons: Use dried eel fish powder and take it on an empty stomach; it can lead to recovery in three to five doses. Alternatively, burn it until fragrant, and consuming it is particularly good. The fish with five-colored patterns is the best.

For abdominal pain caused by poison, a secret method from the high physician: Take one pig liver and one liter of honey, simmer together and divide into twenty doses; or make into pills to take.

To resolve the hundred poisons: Hot drink made from white duck's blood.

For abdominal pain from poison: Burned male cat feces, take with water.

For being afflicted by malicious poison: Grind the intestines of a fox from the twelfth lunar month into powder and take with water, about the size of a thumb.

For malicious poison: Take a piece of grease the size of an egg yolk, dissolve in wine to drink.

For ailments from toad poison and tadpole poison, with feelings of fullness in the chest and abdomen, thirst for water, inability to eat, and restless heavy breathing: Take half a pound of grease, and gradually consume it; the poison will be expelled.[23p]

　　解中蛊毒：生羊肺一具，割开，入雄黄、麝香等分吞之。 【《济生》】
　　解蛊毒：取燕屎三合炒，独蒜去皮十枚，和捣丸梧子大，每服三丸，蛊当随利而出。
　　中蛊药毒，虽面青脉绝，腹胀吐血者，服之即活：用蚕退纸烧存性为末，新汲水服一钱。【《卫生方》】
　　解诸蛊毒，不拘草蛊、蛇蛊、蜣螂蛊，其状入咽刺痛欲死：取胞衣一具，洗切曝干为末，熟水调服一钱。【《梅师方》】
　　食中有蛊，腹内坚痛，面目青黄，瘦瘁，淋露骨立，病变无常：铁精丸。铁精乃煅铁炉中如尘紫色，轻者为佳，不拘多少，研末，鸡肝和丸梧子大，食前后，酒下五丸七丸，不过十日愈。【《肘后方》】
　　虫毒蛊毒：雄黄、生矾等分，端午日研化，蜡丸梧子大，每服七丸，念药王菩萨七遍，熟水下。【东坡方】
　　中蛊吐血，或下血如肝：盐一斤，苦酒一升，煎化频服，得吐即愈。 【《小品方》】[24p]

To cure toxic substances from the "gu" (sorcery): Take one fresh sheep's lung, cut it open, and consume it along with equal parts of realgar and musk.

To resolve "gu" toxins: Take three parts of swallow excrement, fry them, add ten cloves of peeled garlic, mix and pound into pills the size of a walnut, take three pills each time, and the "gu" should be released accordingly.

For those poisoned by "gu", even if their face is dark and veins are collapsed, with abdominal bloating and vomiting blood, taking this remedy will bring them back to life: burn silkworm paper to ash, take a penny’s worth mixed with fresh water to consume.

To dispel all types of "gu" toxins, whether from plant "gu", snake "gu", or dung beetle "gu", presenting as a painful throat condition: Take one piece of fetal membrane, wash, cut, and dry, then grind into powder, mix with warm water and take a penny's worth.

If "gu" is in the food, resulting in abdominal hard pain, a greenish-yellow complexion, emaciation, and irregular illness: Use iron essence pills. Iron essence is prepared from iron in a furnace until it becomes a fine purple powder; use a suitable amount, grind it into powder, mix with chicken liver into pills the size of a walnut, take five to seven pills with wine before or after meals, and recovery should occur within ten days.

For insect toxin "gu": Mix realgar and native alum in equal parts, grind and combine them on the Dragon Boat Festival, forming pills the size of walnuts; take seven pills each time while reciting the Medicine King Bodhisattva’s name seven times, and consume with warm water.

For those poisoned by "gu" with bloody vomiting or bloody stools resembling liver: Take one pound of salt and one liter of bitter wine, boil and dissolve, and take frequently; if vomiting is achieved, one can be cured.[24p]

　　蛊毒药毒：甘草节以真麻油浸之，年久愈妙，每用嚼咽，或水煎服，神妙。
　　蛇蝎蛊毒：牛蒡子煮汁服之。 【《易简方》】
　　卒中蛊毒，下血如鸡肝，昼夜不绝，脏腑败坏待死者：以蘘荷叶密置病人席下，勿令知之，必自叫蛊主姓名也。【《梅师方》】
　　挑生蛊毒，野葛毒：并以升麻多煎，频饮之。 【《直指方》】
　　岭南有挑生蛊毒，于饮食中行厌胜法，鱼肉能反生于人腹中，而人已死，则阴役其家，初得，觉胸腹痛，次日刺人，十日则生在腹中也。凡胸膈痛，即用升麻或胆矾吐之。若膈下痛，急以米汤调郁金末二钱，泻出恶物，或合升麻、郁金服之，不吐即下。李巽严侍郎为雷州推官，鞫狱得吐方，活人甚多也。
　　岭南里人多于食中毒人，渐不能食，胸背渐胀，先寒似瘴：用都淋藤十两，水一斗，酒二升，煮三升，分三服。毒从小便出。十日慎食毒物。不瘥更服。即马兜铃也。[25p]

Gu Poison: Licorice stalks soaked in true hemp oil for many years yield remarkable effects. It can be used by chewing and swallowing or by decocting in water for consumption, showing miraculous properties.
Snake and Scorpion Gu Poison: Take the decoction of burdock seeds.
Sudden Gu Poison: When there is blood in the stool like chicken liver that does not cease day or night, and the internal organs are failing while awaiting death: place sweet flag leaves secretly under the patient's bed without them knowing; they will surely call the name of the Gu master.
Frog Gu Poison and Wild Kudzu Poison: Both are boiled with ligusticum and drunk frequently.
In Lingnan, there is a Frogs Gu poison administered through meals and dining practices, where fish and meat can return life within a person’s abdomen, resulting in death. Initially, one feels pain in the chest and abdomen, then the next day it stabs at the person, and within ten days, it manifests in the abdomen. For any chest discomfort, use ligusticum or orpiment to induce vomiting. If there is pain below the diaphragm, quickly mix two qian of turmeric powder with rice soup to expel the harmful substances, or combine ligusticum and turmeric for consumption; if not vomited, it will pass down. Vice Minister Li Xunyan, while serving as the judge in Leizhou, acquired this vomiting formula and saved many lives.
In Lingnan, many people suffer from food poisoning, gradually unable to eat, with swelling in the chest and back and initial symptoms resembling malaria: use ten taels of Dulin vine, one dou of water, and two sheng of wine, boil down to three sheng, and divide into three doses. The poison will be expelled through urination. Be cautious of poisonous foods for ten days; if not cured, continue the remedy. This also refers to Aristolochia.[25p]

　　中诸蛊毒：王瓜根大如指，长三寸，切，以酒半升渍一宿，服当吐下。 【《外台》】
　　一切蛊毒：饮荠苨汁立出。 【《本草》，下同】　　又方：石蟹热水磨服，自下。
　　又方：霹雳砧一名雷揳，出雷州，并河东山泽间，因雷震处掘地得之，其形不一，有似斧刀者，有似锉刀者，有二孔者，取刮末，服立下。【《雷书》】
　　解中蛊毒：山豆根不以多少，密遣人和水研已，禁声服少许，不止再服。
　　中蛊毒，吐下血如猪肝：茜草根、蘘荷叶各三两，水四升，煮二升，顿服即愈，自当呼蛊主姓名也。【《千金》】
　　中蛊毒：以清油多饮取吐。 【《岭南方》】
　　菜中蛇蛊：蛇毒入菜果中食，令人得病，名蛇蛊。大豆为末，酒渍绞汁，服半升。
　　人头面上有光，他人手近之如火炽者，此中蛊也：用蒜汁半两，和酒服之，当吐出如蛇状。
　　解中蛊毒：胡荽根捣汁半升，和酒服，立下神验。 【《必效方》】[26p]

Poison from Gu: The root of the king melon is as large as a finger, three inches long. Cut it, and soak it in half a liter of wine overnight; taking it will induce vomiting and purging.

Universal Gu poison: Drinking the juice of shepherd's purse will produce immediate results.

Another remedy: Grind stone crabs in hot water and take the mixture to induce a purge.

Another remedy: The thunderstone, also known as the thunder hammer, is found in Leizhou, and in the mountains and marshes of the east of the Yellow River, dug up where thunder has struck. Its shape varies; some resemble axes, some chisels, and some have two holes. Collect the shavings and consume them to induce purging.

For the Gu poison within: The root of mountain beans, regardless of the quantity, is finely crushed and mixed with water. One must consume a small amount in silence, not to stop until more is taken.

For Gu poisoning with symptoms of vomiting blood resembling pig liver: Use three taels each of madder root and artemisia leaves, with four liters of water, boil down to two liters, and drink it all at once to recover. One should also call upon the name of the Gu master.

For Gu poisoning: Drinking plenty of clear oil can induce vomiting.

Snake Gu in food: If snake venom has entered vegetables or fruits, it can make one ill, referred to as snake Gu. Grind soybeans to powder, soak them in wine, and extract the juice to consume half a liter.

If a person has a sheen on their face and another's hand feels hot near it, this indicates Gu poisoning: Use half a tael of garlic juice mixed with wine; consuming it will induce vomiting in a snake-like manner.

To treat Gu poison: Crushing the roots of coriander and extracting half a liter of juice mixed with wine can immediately alleviate the symptoms.[26p]

　　中蛊欲死：马齿苋捣汁一升饮，并傅之，日四五次。
　　卒中蛊毒，或吐血或下血皆如烂肝者：苦瓠一枚，水二升，煮一升，服立吐即愈。　　又方：用苦酒一升，煮苦瓠令消，服之取吐，神验。 【《肘后方》】
　　蛊毒：用东引桃枝白皮烘干、大戟、螌蝥去足翅熬，三物等分为末，以井水服半方寸匕即出，不出更服。或因酒得，以酒服；因食得，以食服。亦可以米泔丸服。【《图经》】
　　中蛊腹痛，面目青黄，淋血骨立：銼枣木心，桑木心亦可，取一斛，水淹三寸，煮至二斗，澄清煎五升，旦服五合，取吐即愈。又煎红水服之，能通经脉。
　　金蚕蛊毒，吮白矾味甘，嚼黑豆不腥者，即是中蛊也：石榴根皮煎浓汁服，即吐出活蛊，无不愈者。【丹溪】
　　解中蛊毒：用未钻相思子十四枚，杵碎为末，温水半盏和服。欲吐，抑之勿吐，少顷当大吐非常。轻者但服七枚神效。【《外台》】[27p]

To counteract the poison from gu (a type of sorcery), if one feels like dying, take one liter of purslane juice, drink it, and apply it to the body four to five times a day.

If someone is afflicted with gu poison and experiences vomiting blood or diarrhea resembling rotten liver: Take a bitter gourd, one full piece, boil it in two liters of water, reduce to one liter, and drink it; they will immediately vomit and be cured. Another method is to use one liter of bitter wine, boil it with the bitter gourd until it dissolves, and drink it to induce vomiting, which is effective.

For gu poison: Use dried white-skinned peach branches from the east, euphorbia, and the cut-off legs and wings of a locust, mixed equally and ground into powder. Take half a tablespoon of this with well water; if it doesn’t come out, take more. If it was caused by alcohol, take it with alcohol; if caused by food, take it with food. It can also be ingested in pill form made from rice wash.

For gu poison causing abdominal pain, a pale or yellow face, and bloody urine: Take the heartwood of jujube or mulberry, one bucket, soak in water to three inches, boil down to two buckets, clarify, and then reduce to five liters; take five doses in the morning and induce vomiting for recovery. Additionally, boiling and drinking the red liquid from it can open the meridians.

If affected by the poison of the golden silkworm, a sweet taste from sucking white alum and chewing non-fishy black beans indicates gu poison: Boil the root skin of pomegranate to make a concentrated juice and drink it to expel the gu, ensuring complete recovery.

To alleviate gu poison, use fourteen unpeeled acacia seeds, crush into powder, and mix with half a cup of warm water. If there’s a desire to vomit, suppress it and do not vomit; shortly after, a significant vomiting will occur. For mild cases, taking only seven seeds is effective.[27p]

　　解中蛊毒：平胃散，以生漆和丸梧子大，每空心温酒下七十丸至百丸。
　　蛊毒百毒，及诸热毒，时气热病，口鼻出血：用人尿尖七枚烧灰，水调顿服，温覆取汗即愈。勿轻此方，神验者也。【《外台》】
　　中诸蛊毒，及六畜肉毒：用伏龙肝末一鸡子大，水服取吐。
　　闽广多蛊，或谓凡至旅寓，当扣主人云：你家有无蛊毒耶？问之即不行。佛说解蛊毒神咒云：姑苏琢，摩耶琢，吾知蛊毒生四角，父是穹窿穷，母是耶舍女，眷属百千万，吾今悉知汝，摩诃萨摩诃。
　　中蛊毒：《梅师方》云，凡中蛊毒，或下血如鹅肝，或吐血，或心腹切痛，如有物咬，不即治之，食人五脏即死。欲知是蛊，但令病人唾于水内，沉者是蛊，浮者非也。用败鼓皮烧灰，酒服方寸匕，须臾自呼蛊主姓名。【《梅师方》】
　　治蛊：取败鼓皮，广五寸，长一尺，蔷薇根五寸，如拇指大，水一升，酒三升，煮二升，服之当下蛊虫即愈。【《外台》】[28p]

To eliminate the poison of Gu: use Ping Wei San, mix it with raw lacquer to make pills the size of a black walnut, and take seventy to a hundred pills with warm wine on an empty stomach.

For all kinds of Gu poison and other heat poisons, as well as seasonal heat illnesses with bleeding from the mouth and nose: use seven pieces of human urine, burn them to ash, mix with water, and take it in one go. Cover to induce sweating for recovery. Do not take this remedy lightly; it is very effective. 【’Wai Tai’】

For the poison from livestock: use powdered liver of a hidden dragon, the size of an egg, mixed with water to induce vomiting.

In Min and Guang regions, where Gu is common, it is advised that when traveling, one should ask the host: “Does your home have Gu poison?” If they inquire, do not proceed. The Buddha’s spell for dispelling Gu poison states: "Gusu Zhuo, Moya Zhuo, I know that Gu poison comes in four corners, the father is the spherical dome, the mother is the woman Yashe, with countless relatives; now I know you all, Maha Saman."

For Gu poison: The ‘Mei Shi Fang’ states that when afflicted by Gu poison, there may be blood in the stool like goose liver, or vomiting blood, or heart and abdominal pain as if bitten by something. If not treated immediately, consuming one’s internal organs will lead to death. To identify the Gu, have the patient spit into water; if it sinks, it is Gu; if it floats, it is not. Use the ash of rotten drum skin and mix it with wine, taking a spoonful to immediately call out the name of the Gu master. 【’Mei Shi Fang’】

To treat Gu: take rotten drum skin, five inches wide and one foot long, and rose root about the size of a thumb, with one liter of water and three liters of wine, boil down to two liters, and take it; the Gu worms will be expelled immediately. 【’Wai Tai’】[28p]

　　蛊毒：用槲树北阴白皮一大握，长五寸，水三升，煮取一升，空腹服，即吐虫出。亦治中蛊下血。【《千金》，下同】　　又方：猬皮灰，水服方寸匕，亦出虫。
　　中蛊吐下血：用榉皮广五寸，长一尺，芦荻根五寸，二味(口父)咀，以水二升，煮取一升，顿服，极下蛊。
　　蛊毒下血，状如鸡肝，日夜不解欲死：桔梗、犀角各等分为末，酒服方寸匕，日三。不能自服，绞口与之。药下心中当烦，须臾自静。有顷下。服至七日止，可食猪脾脏补养。
　　中蛊先下赤，后下黄白沫，连年不瘥：牛膝一两槌散切，以清酒一升渍一宿，平旦空腹服之，再服便愈。
　　　　针灸

　　《千金方》曰：灸蛊毒法，于足小指尖上灸三壮，即有物出。酒饭得之随酒饭出，肉菜得之随肉菜出，即愈神验。皆于灸疮上出。
　　　中毒门

　　　　金匮要略 【汉　张机】

　　　　　禽兽鱼虫禁忌[29p]

Gu Poison: Take a large handful of the white bark of the oak tree from the northern shade, five inches long, and three liters of water. Boil down to one liter and take on an empty stomach to induce the expulsion of worms. It also treats internal Gu and bloody stools.

Another Formula: Use the ash of hedgehog skin, take a thumb-sized quantity with water, which will also expel worms.

Vomiting Blood from Internal Gu: Use the bark of the beech tree, five inches wide and one foot long, along with five inches of cattail root. Chew these two ingredients, boil with two liters of water, and reduce it to one liter. Take in one go to effectively purge the Gu.

If blood is expelled resembling chicken liver, with persistent anguish leading to potential death: Use an equal amount of platycodon root and rhino horn, grind into powder. Take a thumb-sized amount with wine, three times daily. If unable to take by mouth, administer through squeezing. The medicine will cause discomfort in the heart before inducing calmness shortly after. There will be an effect within a while. Stop after taking for seven days, and then you may consume pork spleen for nourishment.

For persistent symptoms of expelling red followed by yellow-tinged foam over many years: Take one liang of cow knee, pound into pieces, and soak in one liter of clear wine overnight. Take on an empty stomach in the morning; further dosage will ensure recovery.

Acupuncture and Moxibustion

The "Thousand Gold Prescriptions" states: For treating Gu poison via moxibustion, apply three moxibustion treatments on the tip of the little toe, then something will be expelled. If consuming alcohol or food, it will emerge with them, proving efficacy. This will all manifest from the area of the moxibustion.

Toxic Entrance

"Essential Prescriptions from the Golden Cabinet" – [Authored by Zhang Ji from the Han Dynasty]

Taboos from Animals, Fish, and Insects[29p]

　　凡饮食滋味，以养于生。食之有妨，反能为害。自非服药炼液，焉能不饮食乎？切见时人，不闲调摄，疾灾竞起，若不因食而生。苟全其生，须知切忌者矣。所食之味，有与病相宜，有与身为害。若得宜则益体，害则成疾，以此致危，例皆难疗。凡煮药饮汁以解毒者，虽云救急，不可热饮，诸毒病得热更甚，宜冷饮之。　　肝病禁辛，心病禁咸，脾病禁酸，肺病禁苦，肾病禁甘。春不食肝，夏不食心，秋不食肺，冬不食肾，四季不食脾。辩曰：春不食肝者，为肝气王，脾气败，若食肝则又补肝，脾气败尤甚，不可救。又肝王之时，不可以死气入肝，恐伤魂也。若非王时，即虚，以肝补之，佳。余脏准此。凡肝脏自不可轻啖，自死者弥甚。凡心皆为神识所舍，勿食之，使人来生复其报对矣。凡肉及肝落地不着尘土者，不可食之。猪肉落水浮者，不可食。诸肉及鱼，若狗不食、鸟不啄者，不可食。诸肉不干，火炙不动，见水自动者，不可食之。[30p]

All food and flavors serve to nourish life. If food is harmful, it can cause injury. Unless one resorts to medicinal concoctions, how can one avoid eating? It is evident that people now do not regulate their diets, and illness arises rapidly, as if not caused by food. To preserve one’s life, one must know what to avoid. Some foods are compatible with health, while others are harmful to the body. If one eats what is suitable, it enhances the body; if detrimental, it leads to illness, which can result in danger that is often difficult to remedy.

When preparing medicinal decoctions to detoxify, even if it is said to be an emergency remedy, one should not consume them hot; poisons worsen with heat, so it is better to drink them cold. Liver diseases should avoid pungent foods, heart diseases should avoid salty foods, spleen diseases should avoid sour foods, lung diseases should avoid bitter foods, and kidney diseases should avoid sweet foods. In spring, do not eat foods that affect the liver; in summer, do not eat foods affecting the heart; in autumn, do not eat foods affecting the lungs; in winter, do not eat those affecting the kidneys; and throughout the four seasons, avoid foods that harm the spleen.

It is explained: in spring, one should not eat liver because the liver is dominant, and the spleen is weakened; eating liver would further nourish the liver and exacerbate the spleen’s weakness, making it irreparable. Moreover, when the liver is dominant, one must not introduce stale energy into it, for this could harm the spirit. If it is not the time of dominance, then when it is deficient, nourishing the liver is beneficial. The same applies to the other organs.

One should not eat the liver lightly; if it dies, it is even more critical. The heart, being the seat of consciousness, should not be consumed, so that one can repay their past in the next life. Any meat or liver that falls to the ground without touching dust should not be eaten. Pork that floats in water should not be consumed. All meats and fish, if not eaten by dogs or pecked by birds, should not be eaten. Any meat that is not dried, or moves when roasted over fire, or moves in water should not be consumed.[30p]

肉中有如朱点者，不可食之。六畜肉，热血不断者，不可食之。父母及身本命肉，食之，令人神魂不安。食肥肉及热羹，不得饮冷水。诸五脏及鱼，投地尘土不污者，不可食之。秽饭馁肉臭鱼，食之皆伤人。自死肉口闭者，不可食之。六畜自死及疫死，皆有毒，不可食之。兽自死，北首及伏地者，食之杀人。食生肉饱饮乳，变成白虫。疫死牛肉食之，令病洞下，亦致坚积，宜利药下之。脯藏米瓮中有毒，及经夏食之，发肾病。[31p]

Meat that has red spots like vermilion should not be eaten. The meat of livestock with continuously flowing hot blood should not be consumed. Eating the flesh of one’s parents or vital life source causes unrest in the spirit and soul. Consuming fatty meat and hot soup does not allow for drinking cold water. The organs and fish that do not become contaminated with dust when thrown to the ground should not be eaten. Rotten rice, spoiled meat, and stinky fish harm the body if consumed. Meat from animals that died on their own with their mouths closed should not be eaten. Meat from livestock that died naturally or from disease is toxic and should not be consumed. Animals that died spontaneously with their heads facing north or lying on the ground can kill if eaten. Eating raw meat and drinking milk to satiety turns into white worms. Eating the meat of cattle that died from disease leads to illness and can cause hard accumulations in the body, requiring purgative medicine. Dried meat stored in rice pots may be toxic, and eating it after summer can lead to kidney disease.[31p]

马脚无夜眼者，不可食之。食酸马肉，不饮酒则杀人。马肉不可热食，伤人心。马鞍下肉，食之杀人。白马黑头者，不可食之。白马青蹄者，不可食之。马肉豚肉，共食饱醉卧，大忌。驴马肉合猪肉食之，成霍乱。马肝及毛不可妄食，中毒害人。疫死牛，或目赤或黄，食之大忌。牛肉共猪肉食之，必作寸白虫。青牛肠，不可合犬肉食之。牛肺从三月至五月，其中有虫如马尾，割去勿食，食则损人。牛羊猪肉，皆不得以楮木、桑木蒸炙，食之令人腹内生虫。[32p]

Horses with no night eyes on their hooves should not be eaten. Eating sour horse meat and not drinking alcohol can lead to death. Horse meat should not be eaten hot, as it harms the heart. Meat from under the saddle is lethal when consumed. White horses with black heads should not be eaten. White horses with green hooves should not be eaten. Eating horse meat with pork and becoming overly full can lead to serious problems. Mixing donkey or horse meat with pork results in dysentery. Horse liver and hair should not be carelessly consumed, as they can poison and harm. Cattle that die from disease, showing red or yellow eyes, should not be eaten, as it is a serious prohibition. Eating beef and pork together will certainly lead to white worms. Beef intestines should not be cooked with dog meat. Beef lungs from March to May may contain worms like horse tails; they should be removed and not eaten, as consuming them can cause harm. Beef, mutton, and pork should not be steamed or grilled with paper mulberry or mulberry wood, as it leads to the generation of worms in the stomach.[32p]

啖蛇牛肉杀人，何以知之？啖蛇者，毛发向后顺者是也。羊肉其有宿热者，不可食之。羊肉不可共生鱼酪食之，害人。羊蹄甲中有珠子白者，名羊悬筋，食之令人癫。白羊黑头，食其脑，作肠痈。羊肝共生椒食之，破人五脏。猪肉共羊肝和食之，令人心闷。猪肉以生胡荽同食，烂人脐。猪脂不可合梅子食之。猪肉和葵食之，少气。鹿肉不可和蒲白作羹，食之发恶疮。麋脂及梅李子，若妊妇食之，令子青盲，男子伤精。[33p]

Eating snake and beef is deadly; how can one know this? Those who eat snake, if their hair stands on end, are affected. Mutton with residual heat should not be consumed. Mutton should not be eaten with fish and cheese, as it harms people. The white beads found in sheep hooves, known as "sheep hanging tendons," cause madness if eaten. A white sheep with a black head, if its brain is consumed, causes intestinal abscesses. Eating lamb liver with peppers harms the internal organs. Pork combined with lamb liver causes heart discomfort. Eating raw cilantro with pork causes umbilical rot. Pig fat should not be eaten with plums. Pork and sunflower should be avoided together, as it reduces energy. Deer meat should not be made into soup with wild arum, as it causes sores. Eating elk fat and plums can cause pregnant women to give birth to boys who are blue-eyed and blind, and harm men's vitality.[33p]

獐肉不可合虾及生菜梅李果食之，皆病人。痼疾人不可食熊肉，令终身不愈。白犬自死不出舌者，食之害人。食狗鼠余，令人发瘘疮。妇人妊娠不可食兔肉、山羊肉及鳖鸡鸭，令子无声音。兔肉不可合白鸡肉食之，令人面发黄。兔肉着干姜食之，成霍乱。凡鸟自死，口不闭，翅不合者，不可食之。诸禽肉肝青者，食之杀人。鸡有六翮四距者，不可食之。乌鸡白首者，不可食之。鸡不可共胡蒜食之，滞气。山鸡不可合鸟兽肉食之。雉肉久食之，令人瘦。[34p]

The meat of deer should not be consumed with shrimp, raw vegetables, plums, or other fruits, as it can harm patients. Those with chronic illnesses should avoid bear meat, as it prevents recovery for life. Meat from a white dog that has died without sticking out its tongue is harmful to people. Eating the leftovers of dogs and rats can cause skin diseases. Pregnant women should not eat rabbit meat, goat meat, or the meat of turtles, chickens, and ducks, as it can cause the child to be mute. Rabbit meat should not be eaten with white chicken meat, as it can cause yellowing of the face. Rabbit meat cooked with dried ginger can lead to cholera. Any bird that has died with its mouth open and wings spread should not be consumed. The liver of various birds that appears green can be fatal. Chickens with six flight feathers and four spurs should not be eaten. Black chickens with white heads should not be consumed. Chicken should not be eaten with garlic, as it causes stagnation. Mountain chicken should not be consumed alongside meat from birds or beasts. Eating pheasant meat for a long time can lead to weight loss.[34p]

鸭卵不可合鳖肉食之。妇人妊娠食雀肉，令子淫乱无耻。雀肉不可合李子食之。燕肉勿食，入水为蛟龙所啖。鱼头正白如连珠至脊上，食之杀人。鱼头中无腮者，不可食，食之杀人。鱼无肠胆者，不可食之。三年阴不起，女子绝生。鱼头似有角者，不可食之。鱼目合者，不可食之。六甲日，勿食鳞甲之物。鱼不可合鸡肉食之。鱼不得合鸬鹚肉食之。鲤鱼鲊不可合小豆藿食之，其子不可合猪肝食之，害人。鲤鱼不可合犬肉食之。[35p]

Duck eggs should not be eaten with soft-shelled turtle meat. A pregnant woman who eats sparrow meat will bear a child prone to debauchery and shame. Sparrow meat should not be eaten with plums. Do not eat swallow meat, as it may be consumed by a dragon if it enters water. The head of a fish that is entirely white, like a string of pearls extending to the spine, if eaten, will kill. Fish heads without gills should not be consumed, as they will kill. Fish without intestines and gallbladders should not be eaten. If three years pass without menstruation, a woman will be unable to bear children. Fish heads that appear to have horns should not be consumed. Fish with cohesive eyes should not be eaten. On the sixth day of the lunar calendar, do not eat fish with scales or shells. Fish should not be eaten with chicken meat. Fish should not be combined with cormorant meat. Carp sauce should not be eaten with mung bean sprouts; its seeds should not be eaten with pig liver, as it harms people. Carp should not be eaten with dog meat.[35p]

鲫鱼不可合猴雉肉食之，一云不可合猪肝食。鳀鱼合鹿肉生食，令人筋甲缩。青鱼鲊不可合生胡荽及生葵并麦中食之。鳅鳝不可合白犬血食之。龟肉不可合酒果子食之。鳖目凹陷者，及厌下有王字形者，不可食之；其肉不得合鸡鸭子食之。龟鳖肉不可合苋菜食之。鰕无须及腹下通黑，煮之反白者，不可食之。食脍饮乳酪，令人腹中生虫为瘕。蟹目相向，足斑目赤者，不可食之。凡蟹未遇霜多毒，其熟者，乃可食之。蜘蛛落食中，有毒，勿食之。凡蜂蝇虫蚁等多集食上，食之致瘘。[36p]

Do not eat crucian carp with monkey or pheasant meat; some say it should not be eaten with pig liver. Anchovy can be eaten raw with deer meat, but it causes contraction in the muscles. Bluefish sauce should not be combined with raw coriander, raw sunflower, or wheat grains. Eels and loaches should not be eaten with the blood of a white dog. Turtle meat should not be eaten with wine or fruits. Turtles with sunken eyes and those with a pattern resembling the character for "king" should not be consumed; their meat must not be eaten with chicken, duck, or goose. Turtle and soft-shelled turtle meat should not be eaten with amaranth. Shrimp without whiskers and with a black underbelly that turns white when cooked are not safe to eat. Consuming raw meat with dairy products can lead to intestinal parasites and lumps. Crabs with eyes facing each other and red spots on their feet should not be eaten. Generally, crabs that have not encountered frost are highly toxic; only cooked ones can be consumed. Spiders that fall into food are toxic; do not eat them. If bees, flies, insects, or ants gather on food, consuming it may result in illness.[36p]

　　　　　果实菜谷禁忌

　　果子生食生疮。果子落地经宿，虫蚁食之者，人大忌食之。生米停留多日，有损处，食之伤人。桃子多食，令人热，仍不得入水浴，令人病淋沥寒热病。杏酪不熟伤人。梅多食坏人齿。李不可多食，令人胪胀。林檎不可多食，令人百脉弱。橘柚多食，令人口爽，不知五味。梨不可多食，令人寒中；金疮、产妇，亦不宜食。樱桃杏多食，伤筋骨。安石榴不可多食，损人肺。胡桃不可多食，令人动痰饮。生枣多食，令人热渴气胀，寒热羸瘦者，弥不可食，伤人。木耳赤色及仰生者，勿食。菌仰卷及赤色者，不可食。正月勿食生葱，令人面生游风。二月勿食蓼，伤人肾。三月勿食小蒜，伤人志性。[37p]

Taboos on Fruits and Grains

Eating raw fruits can cause sores. Fruits that have fallen on the ground for a long time, and those eaten by insects and ants, are very harmful to humans. Dry rice left for many days can be harmful; eating it can injure a person. Eating too many peaches can generate heat, and one must avoid bathing in water, as it can lead to illness with cold and hot symptoms. Unripe apricots can be injurious. Overeating plums damages the teeth. Plums should not be consumed in excess, as they can cause bloating. Eating too many apples can weaken the blood vessels. Consuming excessive oranges or grapefruits will render one unable to distinguish flavors. Pears should not be eaten too much, as they can cause coldness; they are also unsuitable for those with festering sores or postpartum women. Overeating cherries and apricots can harm the muscles and bones. Pomegranates should not be consumed in excess, as they can damage the lungs. Eating too many walnuts can provoke phlegm and fluids. Consuming too many fresh jujubes can cause heat, thirst, and bloating; for those with cold, heat, or emaciation, they should be avoided, as they can be harmful. Do not eat red or sprouted black fungus. Do not eat mushrooms that are rolled or red. In the first month, avoid eating raw scallions, as they can cause facial disruptions. In the second month, avoid eating smartweed, as it can harm the kidneys. In the third month, avoid eating garlic, as it can affect one's spirit.[37p]

四月八日勿食胡荽，伤人神。五月勿食韭，令人乏气力。五月五日，勿食一切生菜，发百病。六月七月，勿食茱萸，伤神气。八月九月，勿食姜，伤人神，十月勿食椒，损人心，伤心脉。十一月十二月，勿食薤，令人多涕唾。四季勿食生葵，令人饮食不化，发百病；非但食中，药中皆不可用，深宜慎之！时病瘥未健，食生菜，手足必肿。夜食生菜，不利人。十月勿食被霜生菜，令人面无光目濇，心痛腰疼，或发心疟，疟发时手足十指爪皆青困委。葱韭初生芽者，食之伤人心气。饮白酒，食生韭，令人病增。生葱不可共蜜食之，杀人。独颗蒜弥忌。枣合生葱食之，令人病。生葱和雄鸡、雉、白犬肉食之，令人七窍经年流血。[38p]

On the eighth day of the fourth month, do not eat coriander, for it harms the spirit. In May, do not eat leeks, as they deplete one's energy. On the fifth day of May, do not eat all raw vegetables, for they cause numerous diseases. In June and July, do not eat bayberries, as they hurt the spirit and energy. In August and September, do not eat ginger, for it harms the spirit. In October, do not eat pepper, as it damages the heart and injures the heart veins. In November and December, do not eat garlic chives, for they cause excessive mucus and saliva. Throughout the four seasons, do not eat raw sunflowers, for they lead to digestive issues and numerous diseases; this applies not only to food but also to medicine, and great caution is advised! When ill and recovering, eating raw vegetables will cause swelling in the hands and feet. Eating raw vegetables at night is not beneficial. In October, do not eat frost-kissed vegetables, as they lead to a dull complexion, watery eyes, heart pain, and backache, potentially causing heart diseases, with blue discoloration of the hands and feet during fever. Eating raw scallions when they first sprout can harm the heart's energy. Drinking white wine and eating raw leeks can worsen illness. Raw scallions should not be eaten with honey, as it can be deadly. Single cloves of garlic are to be avoided. Eating dates with raw scallions can lead to illness. Eating raw scallions with male chickens, pheasants, or white dog meat will cause continuous bleeding from the orifices for years.[38p]

食糖蜜后，四日内食生葱韭，令人心痛。夜食诸姜蒜葱等，伤人心。芜菁根多食，令人气胀。薤不可共牛肉作羹食之，成瘕病，韭亦然。莼多食，动痔疾。野苣不可同蜜食之，作内痔。白苣不可共酪同食，作(上匿下虫)虫。黄瓜食之发热病。葵心不可食，伤人；叶尤冷，黄背赤茎者勿食之。胡荽久食之，令人多忘。病人不可食胡荽及黄花茱。蓣不可多食，动病。妊妇食姜，令子余指。蓼多食，发心痛。蓼和生鱼食之，令人夺气，阴咳疼痛。芥菜不可共兔肉食之，成恶邪病。小蒜多食，伤人心力。扁豆，寒热者不可食之。久食小豆，令人枯燥。食大豆屑，忌噉猪肉。大麦久食，令人作热。[39p]

After consuming sugar syrup, eating raw scallions or leeks within four days causes heart pain. Eating various ginger, garlic, and scallions at night harms the heart. Overeating turnip roots causes bloating. Garlic should not be eaten in stew with beef, as it leads to hard lumps, and leeks are the same. Excessive consumption of water plantain can lead to hemorrhoids. Wild lettuce should not be eaten with honey, as it causes internal hemorrhoids. White lettuce should not be eaten with dairy, as it produces parasitic issues. Eating cucumbers leads to heating illnesses. The core of the sunflower should not be consumed, as it harms one; especially avoid the leaves, particularly the yellow-backed, red-stemmed ones. Long-term consumption of coriander causes forgetfulness. Sick individuals should avoid coriander and yellow flower jujube. Excessive consumption of yam can provoke illness. Pregnant women eating ginger may affect the fetus. Eating too much knotweed causes heart pain. Eating knotweed with raw fish leads to loss of vitality and painful coughs. Mustard greens should not be eaten with rabbit meat, as it causes serious illness. Overconsumption of garlic harms the heart's strength. People with cold or hot conditions should avoid eating broad beans. Long-term consumption of adzukis causes dryness. Eating large bean husks is prohibited if consuming pork. Long-term eating of barley causes heating effects.[39p]

白黍米不可同饴蜜食，亦不可合葵食之。荞麦面多食之，令人发落。盐多食，伤人肺。食冷物，冰人齿。食热物，勿饮冷水。饮酒，食生苍耳，令人心痛。夏月大醉汗流，不得冷水洗着身，及使扇，即成病。饮酒大忌灸腹背，令人肠结。醉后勿饱食，发寒热。饮酒食猪肉，卧秫稻穰中则发黄。食饴多饮酒，大忌。凡水及酒照见人影动者，不可饮之。鲊合酪食之，令人血瘕。食白米粥，勿食生苍耳，成走疰。食甜粥已，食盐，即吐。犀角箸搅饮食沫出及浇地坟起者，食之救人。矾石生入腹，破人心肝，亦禁水。商陆以水服，杀人。葶苈子敷头疮，药或入脑，杀人。水银入人耳及六畜等皆死，以金银着耳边，水银则吐。苦楝无子者，杀人。[40p]

White millet rice should not be eaten with honey, nor should it be combined with sunflower seeds. Eating too much buckwheat flour can lead to hair loss. Consuming excessive salt damages the lungs. Eating cold foods can harm the teeth, and when consuming hot foods, one should not drink cold water. Drinking alcohol and eating raw cocklebur can lead to heart pain. During the summer, if very drunk and sweating, one should not wash with cold water or use a fan, as it may lead to illness. It is a serious mistake to burn the abdomen and back after drinking alcohol, as it can cause intestinal blockage. One should not eat to fullness after drinking, as it can cause chills and fever. Drinking alcohol and eating pork while lying among harvested millet can cause jaundice. Consuming syrup while drinking alcohol is a severe taboo. Any water or wine that reflects a person's moving shadow should not be consumed. Eating fermented food combined with dairy can cause blood stagnation. Eating plain rice porridge and then raw cocklebur can lead to sudden illness. After eating sweet porridge, if one eats salt, it will lead to vomiting. Using a rhino horn chopstick to stir food may expel foam and help save lives if applied to graves. Alum stones consumed may rupture the heart and liver, so they also should not be mixed with water. Consuming the plant Sānglù with water can be lethal. Applying the herb Tínglìzǐ to head wounds can cause the medicine to enter the brain and be fatal. Mercury entering the ear can kill both humans and livestock, and silvers or golds on the ear can cause one to vomit mercury. Bitter neem seeds can be deadly.[40p]

　　　　风俗通 【汉　应劭】

　　　　　论饮食诸毒

　　禽兽自死者，俱有毒，不可食。鱼无腮者有毒，腮大者亦有毒。鳖肚下有红藻纹者，有毒。蟹腹下有毛者有毒。煮酒初出火者有毒，江南谓之火头酒，饮之则生痔溢血。夏月饮食，但过宿者，即有毒。夏月酒在铜锡器中过夜，即有毒。铜气盖热食，气上蒸成汗，滴下食中，即有毒。炊汤过宿，饮之有毒，盥洗则生疥。桃杏仁双仁者，毒能杀人。果未成核者，俱有毒，令人发疮疖。夏秋果熟落地，虫缘者有毒，人食之作漏。屋漏水有毒，人食之有胀而死者；用之沐手，则生浸淫之疥，屡验。泽中死水有毒，饮之令人生瘕。汤池中温泉水不可饮，令人胀闷；惟澡浴可以疏风愈疥癞，盖其泉自硫黄中出，故温也。患疥者宜饱食入浴之，连日数次，汗透而愈。体虚者不可轻浴。[41p]

Customs and Traditions by Ying Shao (Han Dynasty)

On the Poisons in Food and Drink

Animals that die of natural causes are all poisonous and should not be eaten. Fish without gills are poisonous, and those with large gills are also poisonous. Turtles with red algae patterns on their bellies are poisonous. Crabs with hair on their bellies are poisonous. Wine that is just boiled and then removed from the heat is poisonous; in Jiangnan, this is called "firehead wine," and drinking it can cause hemorrhoids and bleeding. During summer months, any food that has been left overnight is poisonous. Wine left overnight in copper or tin vessels becomes poisonous. When food is heated in copper, the vapor rises and condenses into droplets that fall into the food, making it poisonous. Soup that has been left overnight can be poisonous; washing it can lead to scabies. The double almonds of peaches and apricots are deadly poisonous. Fruits that haven't yet formed pits are all poisonous and can cause sores and boils. In summer and autumn, fruits that fall to the ground and are infested with worms are poisonous, causing leakage when consumed. Rainwater that leaks into a house is poisonous; consuming it can cause bloating and even death, and using it for washing hands can lead to scabies, as repeatedly observed. Stagnant water in marshes is poisonous; drinking it can result in abdominal tumors. Hot spring water in baths should not be drunk, as it causes bloating and discomfort; it is only suitable for bathing to relieve skin ailments, since the springs are sourced from sulfur, thus warm. Those suffering from skin issues should eat well before bathing for several days in a row to sweat it out and heal. Individuals with weak constitutions should avoid bathing lightly.[41p]

　　　　千金方 【唐　孙思邈】

　　　　　论五石

　　人不服石，庶事不佳，恶疮疥癣，温疫疟疾，年年常患，寝食不安，兴居常恶，非止已事不康，生子难育，所以石在身中，万事休泰，要不可服五石也。人年三十以上，可服石药。若素肥充，亦勿妄服。四十已上，必须服之。五十已上，三年可服一剂。六十已上，二年可服一剂。七十已上，一年可服一剂。　　又曰：人年五十已上，精华消歇，服石犹得其力。六十已上转恶，服石难得力。所以常须服石，令人手足温暖，骨髓充实，能消生冷，举措轻便，复耐寒暑，不着诸病，是以大须服。凡石皆熟炼用之。凡石之发，当必恶寒头痛心闷，发作有时，状如温疟，但有此兆，无过取冷水淋之，得寒乃止，一切冷食，惟酒须温。[42p]

On the Five Stones by Sun Simiao

People who do not take the stones suffer from various ailments; skin diseases and fevers persist yearly, causing distress in their food and sleep, and their living conditions remain unpleasant. This issue not only affects their health but also complicates childbirth. The presence of stones in the body leads to universal troubles and emphasizes the importance of not taking the Five Stones.

Individuals over thirty may take stone medicine; however, if they are naturally robust, they should not take it recklessly. Those over forty must take it. For those over fifty, they may take a dose every three years; for those over sixty, every two years; and for those over seventy, once a year.

Furthermore, it is stated that those over fifty have diminished vitality, and taking stones can still be beneficial. Yet, for those over sixty, such consumption may lead to adverse effects. Therefore, regular consumption of stones keeps the hands and feet warm, vitalizes the marrow, dispels cold, and improves agility, allowing them to withstand extremes of heat and cold without succumbing to various illnesses; hence the importance of regular intake.

All stones used must be thoroughly refined. If any symptoms arise, they typically manifest as cold-induced headaches or heart discomfort, occurring periodically like intermittent fevers. If such signs appear, do not excessively take cold water but remedy it with warmth, ensuring that all foods are warm, except for wine.[42p]

　　又曰：凡服石人甚不得杂食口味，虽百品具陈，终不用重食其肉。诸杂既重，必有相贼，聚积不消，遂动诸石，如法持心，将摄得所，石药为益，善不可加。余年三十八九，常服五六两乳，自是以来，深深体悉。至于将息节度，颇识其性。养生之士，宜留意详焉！然其乳石必须土地清白光润，罗纹鸟翮，一切皆成白，可入服。其非土地者，慎勿服之。多皆杀人，甚于鸩毒。紫石白石，极须外内映澈，光净皎然，非此亦不可服。寒石五石更生散方，旧说此药方，上古名贤无此，汉未有何侯者行用，自皇甫士安已降，有进饵者，无不发背解体而取颠覆。余自有识性已来，亲见朝野仕人，遭者不一。所以宁食野葛，不服五石。明其大大猛毒，不可不慎也。有识者遇此方，即须焚之，勿久留也！[43p]

It is further said: One must never mix various foods when consuming stone substances. Even if there are a hundred delicacies laid out, do not indulge heavily in the flesh. If mixed too richly, there will inevitably be mutual harm, causing accumulation that does not dissipate, thereby disturbing the stones. If one holds their heart as prescribed, they will achieve what they seek; stone medicine is beneficial, and goodness cannot be enhanced.

In my thirty-eighth or thirty-ninth year, I regularly consumed five to six taels of milk, and since then, I have deeply understood this matter. As for rest and moderation, I have considerable insight into their essence. Those who cultivate health should pay careful attention to this! However, the milk stones must come from clean, pure, and smooth land, with patterns resembling bird feathers; everything must be entirely white to be consumed. As for those not from such land, one should be cautious and avoid them. Many can be deadly, even more so than poison.

Purple stones and white stones must reflect both internally and externally, being clear and bright. If not, they should also not be consumed. The five stones of cold stone are a new formula; this method has been said to not have been known by ancient sages. None among the feudal lords of the Han dynasty have used it. Since the time of the scholar Huanfu Shian, there have been those introducing such potions, yet none have ended well, facing overthrow and collapse.

Since I have become discerning, I have personally witnessed officials from all ranks suffering various fates. Thus, I would prefer to eat wild kudzu rather than take the five stones. It is evident that it is extremely toxic, and one must be cautious! Wise individuals encountering this formula should immediately burn it and not leave it unattended![43p]

　　　　　论解百药毒

　　甘草解百药毒，此实如汤沃雪，有同神妙。有人中乌头、巴豆毒，甘草入腹即定。中藜芦毒，葱汤下咽便愈中野葛毒，土浆饮讫即止。如此之事，其验如反掌，要使人皆知之。然人皆不肯学，诚可叹息。方称大豆汁解百药毒，余每试之，大悬绝，不及甘草。又能加之为甘豆汤，其验尤奇。有人服玉壶丸，致呕不能已，百药与之不止，蓝汁入口即定。如此之事，皆须知之。此则成规，更不须试练也。解毒方中，条例极多，若不指出一二，学者不可卒知，余方例尔。石药毒，用白鸭屎、人参汁。雄黄毒，用防己。铁粉毒，用磁石。礜石毒，用大豆汁、白鹅骨。防葵毒，用葵根汁。大戟毒，用菖蒲汁。桔梗毒，用白粥。甘遂毒，用大豆汁。(艹蹢)(艹躅)毒，用栀子汁。鸡子毒，用淳酢。马刀毒，用清水。野芋毒，用土浆、人粪汁。杏仁毒，用蓝子汁。百药毒，用甘草、荠苨、大小豆汁、蓝叶根实汁。[44p]

On Neutralizing the Poisons of a Hundred Herbs

Licorice neutralizes the poisons of a hundred herbs; this is truly like pouring hot water on snow, and bears a similar mystical quality. If someone is poisoned by aconite or calabash seeds, licorice in the stomach will settle the situation immediately. For those poisoned by rhubarb, swallowing onion soup can quickly remedy it. If one is poisoned by wild yam, simply drinking a mixture of soil and water will stop the effects. Such matters are as clear as turning one's hand over; they should be widely known. Yet, few are willing to learn them, which is truly lamentable.

Soy bean juice is also said to neutralize the poisons of a hundred herbs. In my experience, it is quite limited compared to licorice. Furthermore, it can be enhanced to make a sweet bean soup, yielding even more remarkable results. For someone who takes Jade Pot Pill and vomits uncontrollably, no medicine can stop it, but blue juice taken will immediately resolve the issue. Such knowledge should be recognized. These are established rules, no further experimentation is necessary.

In the realm of antidotes, there are countless regulations; if one does not specify a few, learners cannot fully comprehend. I am merely providing examples: For stone poison, use white duck excrement and ginseng juice. For arsenic poison, use fibrous roots. For iron powder poison, use magnet. For talc poison, administer soy bean juice and white goose bone. For防葵 poison, apply root juice of sunflower. For euphorbia poison, use calamus juice. For balloon flower poison, use white porridge. For cassia seed poison, utilize soy bean juice. (Unclear term) poison, treat with gardenia juice. Chicken egg poison can be neutralized with pure vinegar. For sword grass poison, use clear water. For wild yam poison, employ soil and fecal juice. For apricot kernel poison, take blue juice. The poisons of a hundred herbs can be neutralized with licorice, hyssop, and the juices of large and small beans, and blue leaf root.[44p]

Resolving All Food Toxins

Sesame oil can effectively resolve all food toxins, which should not be overlooked. When preparing dishes, one must first use pure sesame oil in a clean pot to cook until fully heated, then add the meat to stir-fry, and finally, boil it in clean water; this method does not breach any toxicity. In regions like Huizhou and Chizhou, people eat beef daily without regard to spring or summer, primarily due to the proper preparation methods, which results in very few cases of poisoning. For those affected by food toxins, simply drinking one or two cups of sesame oil often induces vomiting and dispels the toxins, leading to recovery in all cases. The best antidote is fire, as fire can transform the properties of substances.[46p]

　　　　　中砒毒

　　世人有服砒霜之毒，五脏欲裂者，腹必大痛，舌必伸出，眼必流血而死，最可怜也。方用泻毒神丹，大黄二两，生甘草五钱，白矾一两，当归三两，水煎汤数碗饮之，立时大泻则生，否则死矣。此砒毒已入于脏，非可用羊血、生甘草上吐而愈，我所以又变下法救之。饮之而不泻，此肠已断矣，又何救乎？倘用之早，未有不生者，不可执吐法而无变通。若初饮砒毒，莫妙用生甘草三两，急煎汤加羊血半碗，和匀饮之，立吐而愈。若饮之不吐，速用大黄之方，则无不可救也。[47p]

Resolving All Poisons

For resolving various medicinal poisons, it is advisable to use juices from shepherd's purse, white hyacinth bean, cowpea, licorice, syrup, rice syrup, and ashes from burnt silkworm paper; all can be used indiscriminately. Withstanding Arsenic Poison

In the world, those who ingest arsenic poison suffer from excruciating pain in their organs, a distended abdomen, protruding tongues, and bleeding eyes leading to death—truly pitiful. The remedy is to use the detoxifying divine pill: two taels of rhubarb, five qian of raw licorice, one tael of alum, and three taels of angelica, boiled in water to make a decoction. Drink several bowls quickly, which will lead to a great purging; otherwise, death will ensue. Once the arsenic has entered the organs, it cannot simply be expelled by sheep's blood or raw licorice. That's why I have created a different method for salvation. If one drinks it without purging, the intestines are already ruptured, and what can be done? However, if used promptly, there is no case of death; one should not rigidly follow the vomiting method without flexibility. If one has just ingested arsenic, it is best to use three taels of raw licorice, urgently prepare a decoction with half a bowl of sheep's blood, mix it well, and drink it for immediate vomiting and recovery. If vomiting does not occur, use the rhubarb remedy quickly, and there’s no reason it cannot be saved.[47p]

二广山谷间，有草曰胡蔓草，又名断肠草，若人以急水吞之急死，缓水吞之缓死，又取毒蛇杀之，以草覆上，以水洒之，数日菌生其上，取为末，酒调以毒人，始亦无患，再饮酒即毒发立死。其俗淫妇人多自配合北人，与人情分相好，多不肯逐北人回，阴以药置食中，北人还，即戒之曰：子某年来。若从其言，即复以药解之，若过期不往，即死矣，名曰定年药。北人届彼，亦宜志之。若觉中毒四大不调，即便服之；或于鸡豚鱼羊鹅鸭等肉下药，复食此物，即触发其毒，急服此药一粒，或吐或利，随服便瘥。昔有一女子久患痨瘵病，为尸虫所噬，磨一粒服之，一时久，吐下小虫千余条，一大者正为两段；后只服苏合香丸，半月遂复如常。至牛马六畜中毒，亦以此救之，无不效。[51p]

Chicken Intestine Grass Powder

This remedy resolves various poisons.

Take three parts of chicken intestine grass, four parts each of shepherd's purse and ginseng, two parts each of peony, angelica, and licorice, one part of vermilion, and one cup of indigo.

Combine these eight ingredients, grind them, and take a dose the size of a thumb with water. It is best to drink plenty of water. If stung by bees or snakes, use a needle to prick the sting site to let blood out, then apply a small amount of the medicine directly into the wound to promote healing. If struck by an arrow, shave bamboo into a point about one foot and five inches long, wrap it in cotton, moisten it with water, and insert into the wound up to the depth of the injury. When good blood flows out, you may stop. If the ingested medicine is toxic, take a dose the size of a thumb with water; it will relieve pain and cure the poisoning.

Detoxifying Powder

Take one part of shepherd's purse and two parts of indigo flower.

On the seventh day of the seventh month, collect indigo, dry it in the shade, grind and sieve it, then mix with water and take a dose the size of a thumb, three times a day.

Alum Ash Powder

For all types of poisons within the body.

Take equal parts of Jinchuan alum and Kuanchan tea.

Grind these into a fine powder, and take two Qian with freshly collected water. If vomiting occurs, it is effective; take again if not.

Indigo and Realgar Pill

For initial signs of poisoning and for snake or insect bites, as well as for early-stage abscesses, take this to prevent the accumulation of toxic gas. Use equal parts of indigo and realgar.[54p]

　　右为细末，新汲水调下二钱。
　　又方　解砒毒。
　　巴豆半粒，用半边，去壳不去白　白扁豆　青黛　甘草　　右同为末，用沙糖一大块，水化开，调一大盏饮之，砒毒随利去，即服五苓散之类。　　又方　解砒毒。
　　汉椒四十九粒　黑豆十四粒　甘草节二寸，碎　乌梅二个　　右(口父)咀，用水一盏，煎至七分，温服。
　　　　单方

　　治自死六畜肉中毒方：黄蘗屑捣服方寸匕。 【《金匮》，下同】
　　治食郁肉漏脯中毒方：郁肉密器盖之，隔宿者是也；漏脯，茅屋漏下沾著者是也。烧犬屎，酒服方寸匕，每服。人乳汁亦良。或饮生韭汁三升，亦得。
　　治黍米中藏干脯食之中毒方：大豆浓煮汁，饮数升即解。亦治狸肉漏脯等毒。
　　治食生肉中毒方：掘地深三尺，取其下土三升，以水五升，煮数沸，澄清汁，饮一升即愈。
　　治六畜鸟兽肝中毒方：水浸豆豉，绞取汁，服数升愈。[55p]

The right is a fine powder, mixed with two coins of freshly drawn water.
Another prescription to resolve arsenic poisoning:
Half a seed of croton, use half, removing the shell but not the white; white hyacinth bean, indigo, licorice. All are to be ground into powder, use a large piece of rock sugar, dissolve it in water, and mix it to drink a large cup; the arsenic poison will be eliminated promptly, then take Five Remedy Powder or similar.
Also, a prescription to resolve arsenic poisoning:
Forty-nine grains of Sichuan pepper, fourteen grains of black beans, two inches of broken licorice root, two black plums. The above should be chewed, boiled with one cup of water, and simmered down to seven tenths, taken warm.

Single prescription:

For treating poisoning from the meat of dead livestock: pound the shavings of Coptis and take a pinch. 【"Jin Kui", the same applies below】
For treating poisoning from spoiled meat and cured flesh: the spoiled meat should be covered tightly; if left overnight, it is so; cured flesh refers to those that have been wet with rain in a thatched house. Burn dog feces, take a pinch with wine each time. Human milk is also good. Alternatively, drinking three sheng of raw leek juice is effective.
For treating poisoning from hidden dried meat in millet: boil a strong broth from soybeans, drink several sheng to resolve. It also treats poison from raccoon meat and cured flesh.
For treating poisoning from raw meat: dig three feet deep, take three sheng of soil from below; with five sheng of water, boil several times, clarify the liquid, drink one sheng to recover.
For treating poisoning from the livers of six livestock or birds: soak fermented soybean curd in water, squeeze out the juice, and drink several sheng to recover.[55p]

　　治马肝毒中人未死方：雄鼠屎二七粒末之、水和，日再服。屎，尖者是。　　又方：人垢取方寸匕服之佳。

　　治食马肉中毒欲死方：香豉二两，杏仁三两，二味蒸一食顷，熟，杵之，日再服。　　又方：煮芦根汁饮之，良。

　　治噉蛇牛肉食之欲死方：饮人乳汁一升立愈。　　又方：以泔洗头，饮一升愈。
　　又方：牛肚细切，以水一斗，煮取一升，暖饮之，大汗出者愈。
　　治食牛肉中毒方：甘草煮汁，饮之即解。
　　治食犬肉不消，心下坚或腹胀，口干大渴，心急发热，妄语如狂，或洞下方：用杏仁一升，合皮研烂，以沸汤三升和取汁，分三服，利下肉片，大验。
　　鸟兽有中毒箭死者，其肉有毒，解之方：大豆煮汁及盐汁服之解。
　　鲙食之在心胸间不化，吐复不出，速下除之，久成症病，治之方：橘皮一两，大黄二两，(石卜)硝二两，三味以水一大升，煮至一小升，顿服即消。[56p]

To treat the liver poisoning in horses when the person is still alive: take 27 grains of male mouse droppings, crush them into a powder, mix with water, and take twice a day. The droppings should be pointed.

Another remedy: take a small amount of human waste and consume it with a spoon.

To treat poisoning from eating horse meat when one feels near death: take 2 liang of fragrant fermented soybean and 3 liang of apricot kernels, steam for a brief moment, mash them, and take twice a day.

Another remedy: drink the juice of boiled reed roots, which is effective.

To treat poisoning from eating snake or beef causing a sense of impending death: drink 1 liter of human breast milk for immediate relief.

Another remedy: wash the head with wash water and drink 1 liter for recovery.

Another remedy: finely chop beef tripe, boil it with 10 liters of water, and reduce to 1 liter, drink it warm; sweating profusely indicates recovery.

To treat poisoning from eating beef: drink the decoction of licorice which will alleviate the symptoms.

To treat indigestion from eating dog meat causing hardening in the chest or abdominal swelling, extreme thirst, and panic with mania: use 1 liter of apricot kernels, crush them together with their husks, mix with 3 liters of boiling water to extract the juice; divide into three servings, which will effectively facilitate digestion.

For birds and beasts that die from poisoned arrows, their meat is toxic: remedy it with juice from soybeans and a saline solution.

For toxicity where fish remains stuck in the chest without digesting, causing vomiting, and leading to chronic illness: use 1 liang of orange peel, 2 liang of rhubarb, and 2 liang of sodium nitrate, boil these three ingredients in 1 large liter of water until reduced to 1 small liter, and take it all at once to eliminate the toxicity.[56p]

　　食鲙多不消，结为症病，治之方：马鞭草捣汁饮之，或以姜叶汁饮之一升，亦消；又可服吐药吐之。
　　食鱼后食毒两种烦乱，治之方：橘皮浓煎汁，服之即解。
　　食鯸鮧鱼中毒方：芦根煮汁，服之即解。
　　食蟹中毒，治之方：紫苏煮汁，饮之三升；或紫苏子捣汁饮之，亦良。　　又方：冬瓜汁饮二升，食冬瓜亦可。
　　食诸果中毒，治之方：猪骨烧过，一味末之，水服方寸匕。亦治马肝漏脯等毒。
　　食诸菌中毒，闷乱欲死，及食枫桂菌而笑不止，野芋烦毒欲死，治之方：人粪汁饮一升，或土浆饮一二升，或大豆浓煮汁饮之，或服诸吐利药并解。
　　蜀椒闭口者有毒，误食之，戟人咽喉气病欲绝，或吐下白沫，身体痹冷，急治之方：肉桂煎汁饮之，或多饮冷水一二升，或食蒜，或饮地浆，或浓煮豉汁饮之，并解。[57p]

Consumption of fish can lead to undigested food that causes symptoms of illness. To treat this condition, one may drink the juice of horse mint, or juice from ginger leaves (one liter), which can also help with digestion; alternatively, one may take an emetic to induce vomiting.

If one experiences discomfort after eating both fish and poisonous substances, the remedy is to drink a strong decoction of orange peel, which will provide relief.

In cases of poisoning from catfish, the treatment is to drink the decoction of reed roots, which will provide relief.

For crab poisoning, the remedy is to drink three liters of boiled juice from perilla leaves; alternatively, juice from crushed perilla seeds can also be effective. Another remedy is to drink two liters of wax gourd juice, or to eat wax gourd.

If poisoning occurs from various fruits, the treatment is to use burnt pig bones, grind them into a powder, and take a small amount (the size of a thumb) with water. This also treats the poison from horse liver slices and similar substances.

For poisoning from various mushrooms, symptoms include distress and near-death experiences, or uncontrollable laughter from eating maple mushrooms, or distress from wild yam poisoning. The remedy is to drink one liter of human feces juice, or one to two liters of soil paste, or to drink concentrated boiled soy juice, or to take various emetic and purging medicines for relief.

If one accidentally consumes Sichuan pepper, causing toxicity and severe throat constriction with symptoms resembling imminent death (such as white frothy vomiting, cold body extremities), immediate treatment includes drinking a decoction of cinnamon, drinking one to two liters of cold water, consuming garlic, drinking earth paste, or drinking strong soy sauce, which will also provide relief.[57p]

　　食躁方：豉浓煮汁饮之。

　　钩吻与芹菜相似，误食之杀人，解之方：荠苨八两，水六升，煮取二升，分温二服。
　　菜中有水莨菪，叶圆而光有毒，误食之，令人狂乱，状如中风，或吐血，治之方：甘草煮汁，服之即解。
　　春秋二时，龙带精入芹菜中，人偶食之为病，发时手背腹满，痛不可忍，名蛟龙病，治之方：硬糖二三升，日两度服之，吐出如蜥蜴三五枚，瘥。
　　食苦瓠中毒，治之方：黍穰煮汁，数服之解。
　　饮食中毒烦满，治之方：苦参三两，苦酒一升半，二味煮三沸，三上三下服之，吐食出即瘥；或以水煮亦得。又服犀角汤亦佳。
　　贪食，食多不消，心腹坚满痛，治之方：盐一升，水三升，煮令盐消，两三服，当吐出食便瘥。
　　凡诸毒多是假毒以投，无知时，宜煮甘草荠苨汁饮之，通除诸毒药。[58p]

Dietary Disorders Remedy: Drink a strong soup made from fermented beans.

The plant called "gouwen," similar to celery, is deadly if ingested by mistake. The antidote is: Eight taels of wild mustard (jili), six liters of water, boil down to two liters, and divide into two warm doses.

The plant "wulangtang" (water hemlock), with round shiny leaves, is toxic. If mistakenly eaten, it causes madness, with symptoms resembling a stroke, possibly leading to vomiting blood. The remedy is: Boil licorice to make a soup, and taking it will bring relief.

During the spring and autumn seasons, a dragon spirit can enter celery; if consumed, it causes illness, leading to swollen backs of hands and unbearable pain, named "Jiaolong disease." The treatment is: Two to three liters of hard candy, taken twice a day, until you expel three to five lizards, and you will recover.

If poisoned by eating bitter gourd, the remedy is: Boil millet to make a soup and take it several times as an antidote.

For general food poisoning and discomfort, the remedy is: Three taels of bitter coptis, one and a half liters of bitter wine, boil together for three rounds, and take it several times until you vomit out the food, leading to recovery; alternatively, boiling it in water will also work. Additionally, rhino horn soup is also effective.

For overeating, which leads to indigestion, swollen abdomen, and pain, the remedy is: One liter of salt, three liters of water, boil until the salt dissolves, take two to three doses, and you will vomit the food and recover.

For all kinds of poisons, many are false poisons thrown at you; if you are unaware, it is advisable to drink boiled licorice and wild mustard juice to help eliminate various toxins.[58p]

　　中砒石乌啄毒：多饮新汲井水，得吐利佳。 【《集简方》】
　　中蒙汗毒：饮井华冷水即愈。

　　中煤炭毒，一时运倒不救：急以清水灌之。
　　卒中水毒，初觉头目微痛，恶寒骨节强急，旦醉夕剧，手足逆冷，三日则虫蚀下部，六七日脓溃，食至五脏杀人也。捣苍耳绞汁服一二升，并以绵染，导其下部。【《肘后方》】
　　中川乌草乌一切药毒，及六畜肉毒：用多年尘壁东土泡汤服之，冷水亦可。 【《通变要法》】
　　中金石药毒：黑铅一斤镕化，投酒一升，如此十余次，待酒至半升顿饮。
　　中轻粉毒：出山黑铅五斤，打壶一把，盛烧酒十五斤，纳土茯苓半斤，乳香三钱，封固，重汤煮一日夜，埋土中，出火毒，每日早晚任性饮。
　　中砒霜毒，烦躁如狂，心腹疼痛，四肢厥冷，命在须臾：黑铅四两，或锡器亦可，磨水一碗灌之。【《危病方》】
　　中硫黄毒：黑锡煎汤服即解。 【《集简方》】[59p]

Poisoning by arsenic: Drinking fresh well water helps induce vomiting and facilitates recovery.

Poisoning by Mongolian sweat: Drinking cold well water results in recovery.

Poisoning by coal: When symptoms occur suddenly without relief, quickly flush with clean water.
Acute water poisoning begins with slight headache and chills, strong bone pain, drunkenness in the morning and evening, with cold extremities. After three days, it leads to parasitic decay in the lower body; after six or seven days, it causes pus formation, potentially fatal to the internal organs. Grind xanthium seeds, extract the juice, and consume one to two liters, also applying it to the lower body.

Poisoning from various toxic plants and animal meats: Use dust from an old wall mixed with Eastern soil in a medicinal bath; cold water is also effective.

Poisoning from mineral medications: Melt one pound of black lead, mix it with one liter of wine, and repeat this process over ten times, drinking half a liter at once.

Poisoning by light powder: Use five pounds of black lead from the mountains, grind it finely, mix it with fifteen pounds of liquor, half a pound of tuber Poria, and three qian of frankincense, seal it tightly, boil in water for a day and night, then bury it in the ground; it is useful for curing fire poison. Drink as desired every morning and evening.

Poisoning by arsenic: Symptoms include agitation, abdominal pain, and cold extremities, life is in peril: Grind four taels of black lead or alternatively use tin utensils, dissolve it in one bowl of water and administer it.

Poisoning by sulfur: Take a decoction of black tin for relief.[59p]

　　中诸药毒：钗子股煮汁服，亦生研更烈，必大吐下；如无毒，亦吐去热痰。
　　中饮食毒：雌黄、青黛等分为末，每服二钱，新汲水下。 【邓笔峰方】

　　山岚瘴毒、疮毒、并中诸毒：锦地罗根研，生酒服一钱匕即解。

　　中诸毒药已死，只要心中温暖者，乃是热物犯之，只用防风一味擂，冷水灌之。 【积善堂方】[60p]

Remedies for Various Poisons:

  1. For symptoms from poisonous herbs: Boil the root of the châi plant, ingest the juice, or grind it for a stronger effect; it will induce significant vomiting and diarrhea. If no poison is present, it will expel heat phlegm.

  2. For food poisoning: Mix equal parts of realgar and indigo into a powder; take two qian (a measurement) with freshly drawn water.

  3. For agitation caused by stone in the breast: Dissolve one qian of Glauber’s salt in honey water and take three times a day.

  4. For poison from foodstuff: Soak four liang (a weight) each of borax and licorice in one jin (a weight) of pure fragrant oil; for those affected by poison, ingest a small cup of the oil, preferably when soaked for a long time.

  5. For miasma and sores: Grind the roots of jǐn dì luó, and take one qian with raw wine, which will provide immediate relief.

  6. For arsenic poisoning: Take two qian of powdered angelica and wash it down with well water.

  7. For arsenic poisoning: Take two qian of powdered curcuma, mix with a little honey, and dissolve in cold water.

  8. For all types of food poisoning: Take one to two qian of cardamom powder, washed down with water.

  9. For symptoms of lead powder ingestion, with bleeding and swelling from the gums: Boil half a liang each of guàn zhòng and huáng lián in water, add a little borneol, and rinse the mouth regularly.

  10. For poisoning from various herbs such as aconite, tian xiong (dormant plant), fu zi (prepared aconite), yan hua (wildflower), and mushrooms: Prepare a decoction of fang feng (siler) and drink it.

  11. If someone has already succumbed to poison, ensure warmth in their heart; if it's heat causing the affliction, grind fang feng thoroughly and wash it down with cold water.[60p]

　　金石药发：麦门冬六两，人参四两，甘草炙二两为末，蜜丸梧子大，每服五十丸，饮下，日再服。【《图经》】
　　食丹药毒：萱草根研汁服之。 【《广记》】
　　丹石发动后，干咳嗽者：每食后饮冬月葵虀汁一盏，便卧少时。 【《食疗》】
　　马汗毒气入腹：葶苈一两，炒研，水一升浸汤服，取下恶血。 【《十全方》】
　　卒中水毒：捣蓝青汁傅头身令匝。 【《肘后方》，下同】
　　服药过剂，烦闷及中毒欲死：捣蓝汁服数升。
　　误吞水蛭：青靛调水饮，即泻出。 【《普济方》】
　　中鼠莽毒：金线重楼根，磨水服即愈。 【《集简方》】
　　一切菌毒，因蛇虫毒气熏蒸所致：芫花生研，新汲水服一钱，以利为度。
　　食雉中毒，吐下不止：用生犀角末方寸匕，新汲水调服即瘥。 【《圣惠》，下同】
　　食物中毒：贝子一枚，含之自吐。又治漏脯毒，面臛毒，及射罔在诸肉中有毒，并用贝子烧研，水调五分服。[61p]

Medical Recipes and Remedies:

  1. Golden Stone Medication: Six taels of Ophiopogon, four taels of ginseng, and two taels of roasted licorice, all powdered together. Form into balls the size of a wutong seed, take fifty balls each time, and drink with water. Take twice daily.

  2. For Poison from Food and Pills: Take the juice of daylily root.

  3. After Taking Dan Stone: For dry cough, drink one cup of winter melon juice after each meal, then rest briefly.

  4. For Horse Sweat Toxic Gas in the Abdomen: One tael of Chinese radish, stir-fried and ground, soak in one liter of water, drink as a soup to expel bad blood.

  5. For Sudden Water Poisoning: Pound indigo and apply the juice on the head and body.

  6. After Taking Overdose of Medicine: For restlessness and symptoms of poisoning, drink several liters of indigo juice.

  7. If Accidentally Ingesting Leeches: Drink water mixed with indigo to induce vomiting.

  8. For Rat Poisoning: Grind the roots of golden thread and heavy building, consume with water to heal.

  9. For All Kinds of Mushroom Poisoning and Toxic Gas from Snakes and Insects: Grind yarrow flowers and mix with fresh spring water, take one qian to facilitate expulsion.

  10. For Primary Symptoms of Poisoning from Eating Quails: Use the powdered horn of a living rhinoceros, mix with fresh spring water, and take for immediate relief.

  11. For Food Poisoning: Keep one shell (of a clam) in the mouth to induce vomiting. Also effective for toxic cured meats and any toxic matter in meat dishes, use the clam shell ground and mixed with water, taking five fen.[61p]

　　中河豚及砒石毒，仓卒无药，急以麻油灌之，多灌取出毒物即愈。 【《易简方》】
　　丹石毒发，发热者，不得食热物，不用火为便，但着厚衣暖卧，取麻油一匙含咽，戒怒二七日也。
　　中野菌毒：急采鸳鸯草啖之，即今忍冬草也。 【《夷坚志》】
　　中一切毒：石菖蒲、白矾等分为末，新汲水下。 【《广记》】
　　中水毒，病手足指冷至膝肘即是：以浮萍日干为末，饮服方寸匕良。 【《集验方》】
　　中鼠莽毒：镜面草取自然汁，青油各一杯，和服，即下毒三五次，以肉粥补之，不可迟。【《医说》】
　　解雄黄毒：防己煎汁服之。

　　中砒石毒：稻草烧灰淋汁，调青黛三钱服。 【《摘要》】
　　一切毒药，及鸩毒，烦懑不止：用甘草三两，水五升，煮取二升，去渣入黍米粉一两，白蜜三两，煎如薄粥食之。【《外台》，下同】
　　乳石发热：乌豆二升，水九升，铜器煮五升，汁熬稠一升，饮之。[62p]

If one is poisoned by pufferfish or arsenic, and there is no medicine available, urgently use sesame oil to flush it out; if enough is flushed, one may recover.

For poisoning by red stone (cinnabar), if there is a fever, one must not eat hot food, and avoid fire. Instead, wear thick clothes to keep warm and lie down, taking a spoonful of sesame oil to hold in the mouth and swallow, abstaining from anger for seven days.

In case of poisoning by wild mushrooms: promptly consume the plant known as "mandarin duck herb," which is now referred to as honeysuckle.

For all types of poisoning: grind acorus calamus and white alum into a powder and take it with freshly drawn water.

For water toxicity, if the hands and feet are cold up to the knees and elbows, take dried floating duckweed as a powder, and ingest a spoonful.

For poisoning by rat poison: extract the juice from mirror grass, combine it with equal parts of blue oil, and take this mixture. Repeat the dosage three to five times, replenishing with meat porridge without delay.

To counteract realgar poisoning: consume the decoction of stephania.

For arsenic poisoning: burn rice straw to ash, mix this with three qian of verdigris, and ingest.

For all poisons, including lethal ones, if there is continuous discomfort: use three taels of licorice, five sheng of water, boil it down to two sheng, remove the residue, and mix one tael of millet flour and three taels of white honey, cooking it until it reaches a porridge-like consistency.

If lacteous stone causes fever: take two sheng of black beans, nine sheng of water, boil in a copper vessel until reduced to five sheng, then concentrate to one sheng and drink it.[62p]

　　中巴豆矾砒鱼肉酒食毒：大豆煮汁饮之。 【《肘后方》】
　　六畜肉毒：小豆一升烧研，水服三方寸匕，神良。 【《千金》】
　　解烧酒毒：菉豆粉荡皮，多食之即解。
　　解鸩酒毒，并诸药毒已死，但心头温者：用菉豆粉三合，水调服。 【《易简方》】
　　解砒石毒：菉豆粉、寒水石等分，以蓝根汁调服三五钱。
　　服石毒发：胡豆半升捣研，以水八合绞汁，饮之即愈。 【《外台》】
　　中砒霜毒：白扁豆生研，水绞汁饮。 【《永类方》】
　　六畜肉毒：白扁豆烧存性研，水服之，良。 【《广记》】
　　诸鸟肉毒：生扁豆末，冷水服之。

　　小虾蟆有毒，食之令人小便秘濇，脐下闷痛，有至死者：以生豉一合，投新汲水半碗，浸浓汁顿饮之，即愈。【《茅亭客话》】
　　服药过剂闷乱者：豉汁饮之。 【《千金方》】
　　服药过剂闷乱，并中草乌、天雄、附子毒；并食饴糖即解。 【《总录》】[63p]

Toxins from various sources and their antidotes:

  1. Poison from middle-sized beans, alum, arsenic, fish, meat, and poisonous food: Boil soybeans and drink the juice.
  2. Meat poison from livestock: Grind one sheng of small beans, take three finger lengths of water to ingest, and it serves well.
  3. To detoxify burnt wine: Use ground mung bean powder liberally, eating more will help.
  4. To counteract poison from deadly wine and other drugs that already killed, especially if there is warmth in the heart: Combine three portions of mung bean powder, mix with water, and ingest.
  5. To counteract arsenic poison: Mix equal parts of mung bean powder and cold stone (cold water stone), and take three to five qian of the mixture with blue root juice.
  6. To expel stone poison: Mash half a sheng of black beans, extract juice by mixing with eight cups of water, and drink it to heal.
  7. To counteract arsenic powder poison: Grind white flat beans and drink the juice.
  8. Meat poison from livestock: Grind roasted white flat beans and take it with water, it works well.
  9. Birds' meat poison: Use raw flat bean powder, and ingest it with cold water.

Small frogs are toxic; consuming them may lead to painful bloating and severe urinary issues, sometimes resulting in death: Take one cup of raw soybeans, soak in half a bowl of freshly drawn water, drink the concentrated juice, and it will heal.
If one has taken excessive medicine resulting in confusion: Drink soybean juice.
If one has overdosed and feels disoriented, and has consumed plant Aconite or other toxic herbs; eating syrup will resolve the issue.[63p]

　　中砒石毒：饮酽酢得吐即愈，不可饮水。亦治食鸡子毒。 【《广记》】
　　狼烟入口：以酢少许饮之。 【秘方】
　　解金银毒：葱白煮汁饮之。 【《外台》】
　　解钩吻毒，面青口噤欲死：以葱涕啖之即解。 【《千金》】
　　郁肉脯毒：杵薤汁服二三升，良。 【葛洪方】
　　食蟹中毒：干蒜煮汁饮之。 【《集验方》】
　　闭口椒毒：气闭欲绝者，煮蒜食之。
　　食诸肉毒，吐下血不止，痿黄者：胡荽子一升，煮令发裂，取汁冷服半升，日夜各一服即止。【《食疗》】
　　食鱼中毒：冬瓜汁饮之，良。 【《小品方》】
　　解狼毒毒：杏仁捣烂，水和服之。 【《千金》】
　　硫黄毒发，令人背髆疼痛，目暗漠漠：乌梅肉焙一两，沙糖半两，浆水一大盏，煎七分呷之。【《总录》】
　　中水毒病，初起头痛恶寒，心烦拘急，旦醒夕剧：梅叶捣汁三升饮之良。
　　食椒闭气：京枣食之即解也。 【《百一》】[64p]

  • For arsenic poisoning: drinking strong vinegar will cause vomiting, after which one should recover; do not drink water. It also treats chicken egg poisoning.

  • For wolf smoke poisoning: drink a little vinegar.

  • To counteract gold and silver poisoning: drink the juice of boiled spring onions.

  • To detoxify from the poison of the fishhook, causing bluish face and difficulty speaking: eat onion mucus to relieve it.

  • For the toxicity of cured meat: crush garlic and drink two to three sheng of the juice, which is effective.

  • For crab poisoning: drink the boiled juice of raw garlic.

  • For spicy pepper poisoning, with suffocation: boil garlic and eat it.

  • For the poisoning from various meats, accompanied by persistent vomiting and hemoptysis: take one sheng of coriander seeds, boil until cracked, then drink half a sheng of juice, once in the morning and once at night to stop it.

  • For fish poisoning: drinking winter melon juice is effective.

  • To detoxify from wolf poison: pound apricot kernels and mix with water to consume.

  • For sulfur poisoning, causing pain in the back and dim vision: roast one tael of black plum flesh, mix with half a tael of sand sugar and one large cup of water, and boil down to seven parts to drink.

  • For water poison symptoms, initially causing headache, chills, agitation, and worsening in the evening: drink three sheng of the juice from plum leaves.

  • For choking from pepper: eating Jujube will relieve it.[64p]

　　中水毒病，初起头痛恶寒，拘急心烦：用梨叶一把捣烂，以酒一盏搅饮之。 【《箧中集》】
　　中桐油毒：干柿饼食之。

　　中砒毒，心腹绞痛，欲吐不吐，面青肢冷：用杨梅木皮煎汤二三碗，服之即愈。 【《易简方》】
　　解诸中毒：芽茶、白矾等分碾末，冷水调下。 【《简要方》】
　　食蟹中毒：生藕汁饮之。 【《圣惠方》】
　　中砒石毒：桐油三升灌之，吐即毒解。
　　鼠莽砒毒：乌桕根半两，擂水服之。 【《医方大成》】
　　解中药毒：巴豆去皮不去油，马牙硝等分研细，冷水服一弹丸。
　　解百毒气：桑白皮汁一合服之，须臾吐利自出。 【《肘后方》】
　　解丹石毒，发热困笃：肥猪肉五斤，葱、薤各半斤，煮食，或作臛食，必腹鸣毒下，以水淘看沙石尽，则愈。【《千金翼》】
　　服石发热：猪肾脂一具，勿中水，以火炙取汁，每服三合，日夜五六服，毒随大便下。【《总录》】[65p]

For poisoning from water: Initially presents with headache and chills, along with a tense and irritable heart. Use a handful of pear leaves, crush them, and mix with a cup of wine to drink.

For poisoning from tung oil: Consume dried persimmon cakes.

For arsenic poisoning, with sharp stomach pain, nausea without vomiting, face turning blue and limbs cold: Boil two or three bowls of juice from the skin of the bayberry tree and take it, which will cure you.

For detoxifying various poisons: Grind芽茶 and white alum into a fine powder and mix with cold water to ingest.

For crab poisoning: Drink fresh lotus root juice.

For poisoning from arsenic: Administer three sheng of tung oil; vomiting will help eliminate the poison.

For poisoning from mouse poisonous grass: Use half a tael of black jujube root, crush with water and take it.

For detoxifying traditional herbal medicine poison: Take the outer skin off the croton seed without removing the oil, finely grind it with white vitriol, and take a pill with cold water.

For detoxifying all poisoned gases: Take one part mulberry bark juice; shortly after, there will be spontaneous vomiting and diarrhea.

For detoxifying cinnabar and stone poison, with fever and extreme fatigue: Boil five jins of fatty pork with half a jin each of green onions and garlic; eat it or make it into an extract, and it must cause rumbling in the stomach to expel the poison; rinse with water to check for sand and stones to ensure recovery.

For heat from stones: Use one pig kidney; do not let it come into contact with water, roast it over a fire to extract the juice, take three he, and consume five to six doses day and night, allowing the poison to be expelled with stools.[65p]

　　食金中毒已死：取鸡矢半升，水淋取汁一升，饮之，日三。 【《肘后方》】
　　解野葛毒已死者：挖开口灌鸡子三枚，须臾吐出野葛，乃苏。 【《肘后方》】
　　胡蔓野毒即断肠草，一叶入口，百窍流血，惟急取凤凰胎，即鸡卵抱未成雏者，已成者不用，研烂和麻油灌之，吐出毒物，乃生，少迟即死。【《卫生方》】
　　闭口椒毒气欲绝，或出白沫，身体冷：急煎桂汁服之，多饮新汲水二三升。 【《梅师方》】
　　乳石热毒壅闭，头痛口干，便漩赤少者：用蜂房煮汁五合服，乳石末从小便中下大效。《图经》云：用十二分炙，以水二升煮八合，分服。
　　药毒上攻：如圣散。用蜂房、甘草等分，麸炒黄色，去麸为末，水二碗，煎八分，临卧顿服，明日取下恶物。【经验方】
　　中诸菜毒，发狂吐下欲死：用鸡矢烧末，水服方寸匕。 【葛氏方】[66p]

  1. For poisoning from gold ingestion, take half a sheng of chicken droppings, extract one sheng of juice with water, and drink it three times a day.

  2. To neutralize the poison from wild kudzu causing death: open the mouth and administer three eggs, and soon the wild kudzu will be expelled, resulting in recovery.

  3. The poison from Hu-man wild herb (also known as bitter cress) causes severe intestinal distress; ingesting one leaf causes blood to flow from all orifices. Urgently take the embryonic form of a phoenix, which is an unhatched chicken egg. The hatched ones are not usable. Mash it and mix with sesame oil for administration; expel the poison for survival. Delay may lead to death.

  4. If suffering from the pepper poison causing respiratory distress or white foam at the mouth, with a cold body, urgently boil cinnamon juice and consume it, drinking two to three liters of freshly drawn water.

  5. For the heat and poison of milk stones causing blockage, with symptoms of headache, dry mouth, and scant red urination: boil five he of bee hives and take the liquid. The powdered milk stones will effectively pass through urine. According to “Illustrated Treatises,” use twelve parts roasted with water to boil eight he, and take in divided doses.

  6. If experiencing adverse effects from medicinal poisoning: e.g., using holy powder, take equal parts of bee hives and licorice, fry the bran to yellow, separate the bran into powder, using two bowls of water to boil down to eight portions. Take this before sleeping, and the next day expel the harmful substances.

  7. For poisoning from vegetable consumption causing madness, vomiting, and severe discomfort: burn chicken droppings to a powder and take it with a spoonful of water.[66p]

　　解一切毒：母猪屎水和服之。 【《千金》】
　　丹石发毒，头眩耳鸣，恐惧不安：淡竹频服二三升。 【《录验》】
　　硫黄毒发气闷：用羊血热服一合，效。 【《圣惠》】
　　解蜀椒毒：鸡毛烧烟吸之，并水调一钱服之。 【《千金》】
　　诸毒卒恶热闷欲死者：新屎汁，水和服；或干者烧末，渍汁饮。名破棺汤。 【苏恭】
　　合口椒毒：人尿饮之。 【《肘后方》】
　　解诸菜毒：小儿尿和乳汁，服二斗。 【《海上方》】
　　自死肉毒：故头巾中垢一钱，热水服取吐。
　　鹧鸪肉，主治岭南野葛菌子毒，生金毒，及温疟久病欲死者，合毛熬酒渍服之，或生捣汁服，最良。【《唐本》】
　　食蟹致伤：丁香末，姜汤服五分。 【《证治要诀》】
　　中河豚毒：五倍子、白矾末等分，以水调下。 【《广记》】
　　中诸药毒：用蚕纸数张，烧灰，冷水服。 【《易简方》】[67p]

To counter all poisons: take the water from pig manure mixed with other substances.
For the toxicity from madder stones, which causes dizziness and ear ringing, along with feelings of fear and unrest: consume two to three sheng of thin bamboo frequently.
For sulfur toxicity causing a feeling of tightness: take a dose of warm sheep's blood, and it will be effective.
To counter the toxicity of Sichuan pepper, inhale the smoke from burnt chicken feathers and also mix a qian with water to ingest.
For severe toxicity with heat, discomfort, and a desire to die: take fresh stool juice mixed with water; alternatively, if dry, burn it to a powder and steep it in juice to drink. This is known as "coffin-breaking soup."
For the toxicity of pepper: drink human urine.
To counter all vegetable poisons: mix a child's urine with milk, and consume two dou.
For the poisoning from decaying flesh: take a qian of dirt from a headscarf, and consume it with hot water to induce vomiting.
Partridge meat is effective against the toxin of wild kudzu mushrooms from Lingnan, the poison of gold, and for those severely ill from intermittent fevers; either stew with fur and drink the wine or crush and drink the juice, which is best.
For injury from eating crabs: take half a liang of clove powder mixed with ginger soup.
For poisoning from pufferfish: use equal parts of gallnut and white alum, mix with water and consume.
For poisoning from various medicines: take several pieces of silkworm paper, burn them to ash, and drink with cold water.[67p]

　　有人服伏火丹药，多脑后生疮，热气冉冉而上，一道人教灸风市数十壮而愈。仍时复作，又教以阴炼秋石，用大豆黄卷煎汤下遂愈，和其阴阳也。【《清明余话》】
　　饮食中毒烦满：苦参三两，(口父)咀，以酒二升半，煮取一升，顿服即吐，愈。【《千金》，下同】
　　食百物中毒：掘厕旁地深一尺，以水满坑中，取厕筹七枚，烧令烟，以投坑中，乃取水汁饮四五升即愈。急者不可得，但掘地着水，即取饮之。　　又方：含贝子一枚，须臾吐食物，瘥。
　　食六畜肉中毒：各取六畜干屎为末，水服佳。若是自死六畜肉毒，水服黄蘗末方寸匕，须臾服与佳。
　　诸食中毒：饮黄龙汤及犀角汁无不治也。饮马尿亦良。
　　中药毒者：取秦燕毛二七枚烧灰服。
　　中野葛毒已死口噤者：取青竹去两节，注两胁脐上，内冷水注之，暖即易。须臾口开，开即服药，立活。惟须数易水。
　　腹中有铁，取白折铁刮取末，井华水服三钱，不过再服。
[68p]

There are those who take fire elixirs, resulting in sores behind their heads, with heat gradually rising. A person taught them to cauterize wind at the market several dozen times, and they were cured. However, it recurred, so they were taught to refine autumn stones with Yin energy, boiling them with soybeans to create a decoction for consumption, thus achieving balance in Yin and Yang.

For food poisoning with fullness and discomfort: take three taels of bitter realgar, chew it, mix with two and a half sheng of wine, boil down to one sheng, and take it all at once; this will induce vomiting and cure the ailment.

For poisoning from eating various foods: dig a pit beside the latrine about one foot deep, fill it with water, take seven pieces of latrine wood, burn them to create smoke, and throw them into the pit. Then drink four to five sheng of the water; this will cure you. If in urgent need and unable to find wood, simply dig a hole and use the water to drink.

Another method: hold one piece of shell, and after a moment, vomit the food to recover.

For poisoning from meat of six animals: take the dried feces of the six animals and grind it into powder to take with water. If the meat comes from an animal that died naturally, take a specific measurement of huangbai (barberry) powder mixed with water, and taking it shortly will provide relief.

For poisoning from various foods: drinking Huanglong soup and rhino horn juice cures all. Drinking horse urine is also good.

For poisoning from certain medicines: take two to seven pieces of Qin swallow feathers, burn them to ash, and consume.

For those poisoned by wild kudzu who have died and cannot open their mouths: take a green bamboo, removing two nodes, and inject cold water into the sides and above the navel. When it warms, it will change. In a moment, the mouth will open, and when it opens, take medicine immediately, and recovery will be instant. Just be sure to change the water several times.

If there is iron in the belly, take white broken iron and scrape it to obtain powder, and consume three qian with well water, repeating no more than twice.[68p]
